 Stephan: Hello guys!
The WÃ¼rzburg International Network (WIN) is a group of volunteers organizing events and free time activities for exchange students to make it easier for you to connect, create memories, and have a good time. Usually we meet every other week in order to plan upcoming activities. We are always open for new members and supporters no matter where you come from and what you study.  Stephan: No. It depends on several parameters. And it depends on what kind of tax you mean. You'll be taxed for healthcare, retirement, unemployment etc. but probably there wont be an income tax.
 ~â€¯Alex: Lets start from the scratch. 
- In Germany Yearly you can each 10.908 Euros without paying tax. Everything that is bigger will be taxed. 
- Second of all anyway you will pay around 9% for pension tax
 ~â€¯Alex: *earn
 ~â€¯Bengisu Kaya: Thank you
 ~â€¯Alex: Third important: students working hours in sum should not be higher than full-time worker for half a year(so we can say that students can work only half a year full time)

 ~â€¯Alex: So if you work in a big company and the company offers it: ask your managers to pay for your:
-tickets
-car in leasing
-invest in stocks 
from your salary before the taxes are applied. But I am not sure they will do it for working students.
 Stephan: If you work as a student you have two options: Be employed as a student (Werkstudent) - pay less social tax, take care of health care yourself. Or be employed as an employee (Arbeitnehmer) - more social tax but health care is included.

 ~â€¯Saleh: Take Dogs and Other Pets with You
Do you want to bring your dog and other pets on your journey? Simply book online or through the app here.
Note: Dogs that do not travel in a transport box must be leashed and wear a muzzle.

Your Benefits
For small dogs and other small pets (up to the size of a house cat), you don't need a ticket if the animals are carried in a suitable transport container.
For larger dogs, you need a separate ticket. You only pay half the fare.
Dogs that do not travel in a transport box must be leashed and wear a muzzle.
Guide dogs for the blind and marked assistance dogs always travel free of charge and do not need to wear a muzzle on the train.

 ~â€¯Anthony: Deutschlandticket special offer for WÃ¼rzburg students!

Starting 1 October 2023, you can travel by local trains & buses all across Germany with the Deutschlandticket for a special price of only â‚¬15 per month for WÃ¼rzburg students! This is optional on top of the â‚¬14 per month you are required to pay for the semester ticket within the VVM service area (WÃ¼rzburg & the surrounding areas)

*If you already have an existing regular Deutschlandticket subscription, you must unsubscribe it first before the 10th of the final month you're using it, as the ticket type cannot be automatically changed.*

You can only buy this ticket online from either the *WVV app* using evidence of an immatriculation certificate, or the *Deutschlandticket Mainfranken website* using login with your online credentials & have your ticket saved in Google or Apple Wallet on your device. It is NOT obtainable from ticket machines, bus drivers, or other operators.

How to buy from WVV:
1. Download the "WVV mobil" app or open the "WVV Webshop" on your browser.
2. Create an account, then input your payment method (currently accepts auto debit from either a European/SEPA bank account, credit card, or Paypal).
3. Once you are logged in, go to the "Deutschlandticket" menu, choose the "Deutschlandticket Studium" that costs â‚¬15 per month. On the next page, choose the month of when you want to start the subscription, then click the word "click here". It will lead you to another page where you can upload your *immatriculation certificate* from one of the WÃ¼rzburg colleges: Uni WÃ¼rzburg, THWS, Hochschule fÃ¼r Musik.
4. You will receive an email from WVV within 3 working days regarding your eligibility. The ticket can then finally be purchased from the same page.
5. Your ticket can then at anytime be accessed through the "Pinboard" menu in the app.

The ticket allows you to take all local public transports within Germany and a few steps beyond the borders. It is not valid on first class, the ICE fast trains & private operators (e.g. Flixbus/Flixtrain). The ticket is NOT transferable (i.e. other people cannot use your ticket, as you may be required to show an ID that has the same name as on the ticket.) and you can only have one ticket per device.

6. Regardless of the date of purchase, the ticket is valid for the whole calendar month stated until 3AM on the 1st day of the following month.
7. The ticket renews automatically for the following month. If you wish to stop using it, don't forget to click "unsubscribe now" at the bottom of the ticket page by the 10th of the final month you will be using it.
8. If you are staying for more than one semester, you will be required to upload a new immatriculation certificate for the following semester(s), when prompted to do so.

Have a happy & safe travels around Germany!

Disclaimer: Information here may change at anytime without notice. And of course, this post is not sponsored, but solely extracted based on the information available in German.

 ~â€¯Anthony: *A quick reminder...if you want to travel around Germany using the Deutschlandticket for a reduced rate of â‚¬15/month and start using it from 1 October (this Sunday), you need to buy it using the WVV mobil app & provide your student immatriculation & be verified by then. You can already buy the tickets now if you had been verified. Here's how to buy it:*

*Deutschlandticket special offer for WÃ¼rzburg students!*

Starting 1 October 2023, you can travel by local trains & buses all across Germany with the Deutschlandticket for a special price of only â‚¬15 per month for WÃ¼rzburg students! This is optional on top of the â‚¬14 per month you are required to pay for the semester ticket within the VVM service area (WÃ¼rzburg & the surrounding areas)

*If you already have an existing normal rate Deutschlandticket subscription, you must unsubscribe it first before the 10th of the final month you're using it, as the ticket type cannot be automatically changed and so that you will not be double charged for the following month.*

You can only buy this ticket online, either from the *WVV mobil app* using evidence of an immatriculation certificate, or the *Deutschlandticket Mainfranken website* using login with your online credentials & then have your ticket saved in Google or Apple Wallet on your device. It is NOT available in ticket machines or counters, bus drivers, or other operators.

How to buy from WVV mobil:
1. Download the *WVV mobil* app or open the "WVV Webshop" (ticketswvv.de) on your browser.
2. Create an account, then input your payment method (currently accepts auto debit from either a European/SEPA bank account, a credit card, or Paypal).
3. Once you are logged in, go to the "Deutschlandticket" menu, choose the "Deutschlandticket Studium" that costs â‚¬15 per month. On the next page, choose the month of when you want to start the subscription, then click the word "click here". It will lead you to another page where you can upload your *immatriculation certificate* from one of the WÃ¼rzburg colleges: Uni WÃ¼rzburg, THWS, Hochschule fÃ¼r Musik.
4. You will receive an email from WVV within 3 working days regarding your eligibility. The ticket can then finally be purchased from the same page.
5. Your ticket can then at anytime be accessed through the "Pinboard" menu in the app.

The ticket allows you to take all local public transports within Germany and a few steps beyond the borders. It is NOT valid on the ICE fast trains & private operators (e.g. Flixbus/Flixtrain). The ticket is NOT transferable (i.e. other people cannot use your ticket, as you may be required to show an ID that has the same name as on the ticket.) and you can only have one ticket per device.

6. Regardless of the date of purchase (you can buy from 3 months before the validity begins), the ticket is valid for the whole calendar month as stated, from midnight on the first day until 3AM on the 1st day of the following month.
7. The ticket renews automatically for the following month. If you wish to stop using it, don't forget to click "unsubscribe now" at the bottom of the ticket page by the 10th of the final month you will be using it.
8. If you are staying for more than one semester, you will need to upload a new immatriculation certificate for the following semester(s), when prompted to do so.

Have a happy & safe travels around Germany!
